  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Select group infomation of groups I belong Select "group"."group_id" , "name", "information", TYPE from "user_in_group" INNER JOIN "group" on "user_in_group"."group_id" = "group"."group_id" where "user_id" = 2; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('user') WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('post') WHEN "t3"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('event') END as "content_type", "t1"."name" , "user_id" , "regular_user_id" , "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "t2"."date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type" FULL JOIN (Select "information" , text('event') as "content_type" from "event" where "event"."name" LIKE '%ia%' or "event"."information" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t3" on "t2"."content_type" = "t3"."content_type";

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Select group infomation of groups I belong Select "group"."group_id" , "name", "information", TYPE from "user_in_group" INNER JOIN "group" on "user_in_group"."group_id" = "group"."group_id" where "user_id" = 2; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('user') WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('post') END as "content_type", "t1"."name" , "user_id" , "regular_user_id" , "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "t2"."date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type" FULL JOIN (Select "information" , text('event') as "content_type" from "event" where "event"."name" LIKE '%ia%' or "event"."information" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t3" on "t2"."content_type" = "t3"."content_type";

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Select group infomation of groups I belong Select "group"."group_id" , "name", "information", TYPE from "user_in_group" INNER JOIN "group" on "user_in_group"."group_id" = "group"."group_id" where "user_id" = 2; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('user') WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('post') END as "content_type", "name" , "user_id" , "regular_user_id" , "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type" FULL JOIN (Select * from "event" where "event"."name" LIKE '%ia%' or "event"."information" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t3" on "t2"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type";

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Select group infomation of groups I belong Select "group"."group_id" , "name", "information", TYPE from "user_in_group" INNER JOIN "group" on "user_in_group"."group_id" = "group"."group_id" where "user_id" = 2; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN "t1"."content_type" WHEN "t4"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN "t4"."content_type" END as "content_type", "t1"."name" , "user_id" , "regular_user_id" , "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "t2"."date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN ( Select CASE WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN "t2"."content_type" WHEN "t3"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN "t3"."content_type" END as "content_type", * from (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" FULL JOIN (Select "information" , text('event') as "content_type" from "event" where "event"."name" LIKE '%ia%' or "event"."information" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t3" on "t2"."content_type" = "t3"."content_type" ) as "t4" on "t1"."content_type" = "t4"."content_type";

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('user') WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('post') WHEN "t3"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('event') END as "content_type", "t1"."name" , "user_id" , "regular_user_id" , "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "t2"."date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN ( Select * from (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" FULL JOIN (Select "information" , text('event') as "content_type" from "event" where "event"."name" LIKE '%ia%' or "event"."information" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t3" on "t2"."content_type" = "t3"."content_type" ) as "t4" on "t1"."content_type" = "t4"."content_type";

--Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('user') WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('post') WHEN "t3"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('event') END as "content_type", "t1"."name" , "user_id" , "regular_user_id" , "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "t2"."date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type" FULL JOIN (Select "information" , text('event') as "content_type" from "event" where "event"."name" LIKE '%ia%' or "event"."information" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t3" on "t2"."content_type" = "t3"."content_type";

Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('user') WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('post') END as * from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type" FULL JOIN (Select "information" , text('event') as "content_type" from "event" where "event"."name" LIKE '%ia%' or "event"."information" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t3" on "t2"."content_type" = "t3"."content_type";

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('user') WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('post') END as "content_type", "t1"."name" , "user_id" , "regular_user_id" , "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "t2"."date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type"

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Select group infomation of groups I belong Select "group"."group_id" , "name", "information", TYPE from "user_in_group" INNER JOIN "group" on "user_in_group"."group_id" = "group"."group_id" where "user_id" = 2; Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('user') WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('post') END as "content_type", "t1"."name" , "user_id" , "regular_user_id" , "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "t2"."date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type" FULL JOIN (Select * , text('event') as "content_type" from "event" where "event"."name" LIKE '%ia%' or "event"."information" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t3" on "t2"."content_type" = "t3"."content_type";

Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('user') WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('post') END as "content_type", "t1"."name" , "user_id" , "regular_user_id" , "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type" FULL JOIN (Select * , text('event') as "content_type" from "event" where "event"."name" LIKE '%ia%' or "event"."information" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t3" on "t2"."content_type" = "t3"."content_type";

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select CASE WHEN "t1"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('user') WHEN "t2"."content_type" IS NOT NULL THEN text('post') END as "content_type", "name" , "user_id" , "regular_user_id" , "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from (Select "name", "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type" FULL JOIN Select * from "event" where "event"."name" LIKE '%ia%' or "event"."information" LIKE '%ia%';

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2;   • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Select group infomation of groups I belong Select "group"."group_id" , "name", "information", TYPE from "user_in_group" INNER JOIN "group" on "user_in_group"."group_id" = "group"."group_id" where "user_id" = 2; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Select group infomation of groups I belong Select "group"."group_id" , "name", "information", TYPE from "user_in_group" INNER JOIN "group" on "user_in_group"."group_id" = "group"."group_id" where "user_id" = 2; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type";

--Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" INNER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , text('post') as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."content_type" = "t2"."content_type" order by "t1"."content_type";

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Select group infomation of groups I belong Select "group"."group_id" , "name", "information", TYPE from "user_in_group" INNER JOIN "group" on "user_in_group"."group_id" = "group"."group_id" where "user_id" = 2; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body";

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Select group infomation of groups I belong Select "group"."group_id" , "name", "information", TYPE from "user_in_group" INNER JOIN "group" on "user_in_group"."group_id" = "group"."group_id" where "user_id" = 2; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , "post" as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body"; Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , text('user') as "content_type" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%ia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , 'post' as "content_type" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%ia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%ia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body";

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Select group infomation of groups I belong Select "group"."group_id" , "name", "information", TYPE from "user_in_group" INNER JOIN "group" on "user_in_group"."group_id" = "group"."group_id" where "user_id" = 2; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select * from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%dia%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" , 2 as codntent from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%dia%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%dia%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body";

Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ; -- Select all regular users and post with starting name ou title ou body is like something... Select "content" from (Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" , 2 as "content" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE '%para%') as "t1" FULL OUTER JOIN (Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id", 2 as "content" from "post" where "post"."body" LIKE '%para%' or "post"."title" LIKE '%para%' ) as "t2" on "t1"."name" = "body";

  • -- my info Select "user_id", "name" from "user" where "email" = 'jokinho@feup.pt'; -- if is admin Select "admin_id" from "admin" where "user_id" = 24; -- if is regular_user Select "regular_user_id", "personal_info" from "regular_user" where "user_id" = 4; --if is a student Select "student_id" from "student" where "regular_user_id" = 5; -- if is a teacher Select "teacher_id" from "teacher" where "regular_user_id" = 3; -- if is an organization Select "organization_id" from "organization" where "regular_user_id" = 4; -- Select user from a group Select "user_id" from "user_in_group" where "group_id" = 1; --events of organization Select "name", "location", "date", "information" from "event" where "organization_id" = 1; --Posts posted by me Select "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "author_id" = 2; --Notification Select "origin_user_id", "description", "link", "date" from "notification" INNER JOIN "notified_user" on "notification"."notification_id" ="notified_user"."notification_id" where "user_notified" = 5; --Message by chat Select "sender_id", "body", "date" from "message" where "chat_id" = 2 order by "date" DESC; --Comments Select "comment_id", "user_id", "comment_to_id", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes" from "comment" where "post_id" = 5 order by "date" DESC; --Posts from event Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "event_id" = 1; --Posts from group Select "author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", TYPE, "event_id", "group_id" from "post" where "group_id" = 1; -- Select all regular users with starting name like... Select "name" , "user"."user_id" , "regular_user"."regular_user_id" from "user" INNER JOIN "regular_user" on "regular_user"."user_id" = "user"."user_id" where "user"."name" LIKE 'A%'; -- Select Reports that have no answer Select "reporter_id", "approval", "reason", "reported_user_id", "reported_event_id", "reported_post_id", "reported_comment_id", "reported_group_id" from "report" where "approval" IS NULL; --Select friends Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'accepted' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Select pending requests (the user that hasn't answered) Select "friend_id2" from "friend" where (TYPE = 'pending' and "friend_id1" = 2); --Files path from Posts Select "file_path" from "file" INNER JOIN "post" on "post"."post_id" = "file"."post_id" where "post"."post_id" = 7 order by "date" DESC; --Event informations of events I am interested on Select "event"."event_id", "organization_id", "name", "location", "date", "information" FROM "event" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "event"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" Where "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2; --Posts from groups I belong, users I am friends with and events I am interested on (Feed) Select * from ( Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_in_group" on "post"."group_id" = "user_in_group"."group_id" where "user_in_group"."user_id" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "friend" on "friend"."friend_id2" = "post"."author_id" WHERE "friend".TYPE = 'accepted' AND "friend"."friend_id1" = 2 UNION Select "post_id","author_id", "title", "body", "date", "upvotes", "downvotes", "post".TYPE, "post"."event_id", "post"."group_id" from "post" INNER JOIN "user_interested_in_event" on "post"."event_id" = "user_interested_in_event"."event_id" WHERE "user_interested_in_event"."user_id" = 2 ) as posts NATURAL JOIN (Select "post_id",count("post_id") from "comment" GROUP BY "post_id") as "comments" ;
